ChargeVoltsDiv10 ::= TEXTUAL-CONVENTION
    DISPLAY-HINT "d-1"
    STATUS       current
    DESCRIPTION  "Charge Voltage. Fixed point, one decimal"
    SYNTAX       Unsigned32 (0..40)

    DISPLAY-HINT "d-1"
    STATUS       current
    DESCRIPTION  "Frequency. Fixed point, one decimal"
    SYNTAX       Unsigned32 (0..70)

-- ************************************* TRAP/NOTIFICATION MANAGEMENT SECTION *************************************

dse74xxAlarmsMngr OBJECT IDENTIFIER ::= { dse74xx 150 }

dse74xxAlarmStateTable OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX		SEQUENCE OF DSE74xxAlarmStateSequence
	MAX-ACCESS	not-accessible
	STATUS		current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Alarms state table"
	::= { dse74xxAlarmsMngr 1 }
	
DSE74xxAlarmStateSequence ::= SEQUENCE {
	dse74xxAlarmKeyID		Integer32,
	dse74xxSeqNr			Counter32,
	dse74xxTrapID			Integer32,
	dse74xxTrapState		Integer32,
--	dse74xxTrapOrigin		Integer32,
	dse74xxTrapTimeStamp	TimeTicks
}

dse74xxAlarmStateEntry OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX		DSE74xxAlarmStateSequence
	MAX-ACCESS	not-accessible
	STATUS		current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Entry in the alarms state table,
		indexed by Key ID (1..3)"
	INDEX
--		{ dse74xxTrapID }
		{ dse74xxAlarmKeyID }
	::= { dse74xxAlarmStateTable 1 }

dse74xxAlarmKeyID OBJECT-TYPE
  SYNTAX  Integer32 (1..100)
  MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
  STATUS  current
  DESCRIPTION "Notification Key ID"
	::= { dse74xxAlarmStateEntry 1 }

dse74xxSeqNr  OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX		Counter32
	MAX-ACCESS	read-only
	STATUS		current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Alarm sequence number"
--	::= { dse74xxAlarmStateEntry 1 }
	::= { dse74xxAlarmStateEntry 2 }

dse74xxTrapID OBJECT-TYPE
--	SYNTAX		Integer32 (0x1000..0x6FFF)
	SYNTAX		Integer32 (4096..28671)
	MAX-ACCESS	read-only
	STATUS		current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Alarm identification number"
--	::= { dse74xxAlarmStateEntry 2 }
	::= { dse74xxAlarmStateEntry 3 }

dse74xxTrapState OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX		INTEGER {
				alarmNormal (1),
				alarmWarning (2),
				alarmElectricalTrip (3),
				alarmShutdown (4),			
				modeStop (5),
				modeManual (6),
				modeTest (7),
				modeAuto (8),
				modeConfig (9),
				singleEventNotification (10),
				ecuLampOff (11),
				ecuLampFlashSlow (12),
				ecuLampFlashFast (13),
				ecuLampOnSteady (14),
				fuelLevelUsageNormal (15),
				fuelLevelEndFill (16),		
				fuelLevelStartFill (17),				
				fuelLevelUsageTheftAlarm (18),
				fuelLevelUsageLevelAlarm (19)
			}
	MAX-ACCESS	read-write
	STATUS		current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Alarm state. Trap 'alarmNormal' clears former alarms."
	::= { dse74xxAlarmStateEntry 4 }
	
--dse74xxTrapOrigin OBJECT-TYPE
--	SYNTAX		Integer32 (0..100)
--	MAX-ACCESS	read-only
--	STATUS		current
--	DESCRIPTION
--		"Alarm identification origin"
--	::= { dse74xxAlarmStateEntry 4 }
--	::= { dse74xxAlarmStateEntry 5 }
	
dse74xxTrapTimeStamp OBJECT-TYPE
	SYNTAX		TimeTicks
	MAX-ACCESS	read-only
	STATUS		current
	DESCRIPTION
		"Trap timestamp in UNIX format - seconds since Jan 01 1970. (UTC)."
--	::= { dse74xxAlarmStateEntry 5 }
	::= { dse74xxAlarmStateEntry 6 }

dseKeypressTable  OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX  SEQUENCE OF DseKeypressEntry
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS  current
    DESCRIPTION
     "Mains Table"
    ::= { dse74xxControl 1 }

dseKeypressEntry OBJECT-TYPE
    SYNTAX  DseKeypressEntry
    MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
    STATUS  current
    DESCRIPTION
     "Key Press Entry"
    INDEX { keypressKeyID }
    ::= { dseKeypressTable  1 }

DseKeypressEntry ::= SEQUENCE {
  keypressKeyID         INTEGER,
  keypress           OCTET STRING
  }
  
keypressKeyID OBJECT-TYPE
  SYNTAX  Integer32 (1..2147483647)
  MAX-ACCESS  not-accessible
  STATUS  current
  DESCRIPTION "Keypress Key ID"
  ::= { dseKeypressEntry 1 }
  
  
keypress OBJECT-TYPE
  SYNTAX  OCTET STRING
  MAX-ACCESS  read-write
  STATUS  current
  DESCRIPTION "Valid values: ACT_ON, ACT_MAN, ACT_TEST, ACT_AUTO, ACT_OFF, ACT_GEN, ACT_MAINS, ACT_BUZZ, ACT_AL_RESET, ACT_MANRESTORE, NO_ACT"
  ::= { dseKeypressEntry 2 }

MainsEntry ::= SEQUENCE {
	mainsKeyID          Integer32,	        -- Mains frequency
	mainsFreq        	FreqDiv10,	        -- Mains Frequency
	mainsL1Volts        VoltsLNDiv10,	    -- Mains L1-N voltage
	mainsL2Volts        VoltsLNDiv10,	    -- Mains L2-N voltage
	mainsL3Volts        VoltsLNDiv10,	    -- Mains L3-N voltage
	mainsL1L2Volts      VoltsLLDiv10,	    -- Mains L1-L2 voltage
	mainsL2L3Volts      VoltsLLDiv10,	    -- Mains L2-L3 voltage
	mainsL3L1Volts      VoltsLLDiv10,	    -- Mains L3-L1 voltage
	mainsL1Current      CurrentDiv10,	    -- Mains L1 current - Mains L1 current when CT ON LOAD is selected
	mainsL2Current      CurrentDiv10,	    -- Mains L2 current - Mains L2 current when CT ON LOAD is selected
	mainsL3Current      CurrentDiv10,	    -- Mains L3 current - Mains L3 current when CT ON LOAD is selected
	mainsECurrent       CurrentDiv10,	    -- Mains earth current - Mains Earth current when CT ON LOAD is selected
	mainsL1Watts        Integer32,	        -- Mains L1 Watts
	mainsL2Watts        Integer32,	        -- Mains L2 Watts
	mainsL3Watts        Integer32,	        -- Mains L3 Watts
	mainsRotation       Unsigned32,         -- Mains phase rotation
	mainsTotalWatts     Integer32,	        -- Mains Total Watts (hi) *****************************
	mainsL1VA           Unsigned32,         -- 
	mainsL2VA           Unsigned32,         -- 
	mainsL3VA           Unsigned32,         -- 
	mainsTotalVA        Integer32,         -- 
	mainsL1VAr          Integer32,	        -- 
	mainsL2VAr          Integer32,	        -- 
	mainsL3VAr          Integer32,	        -- 
	mainsTotalVAr       Integer32,	        -- 
	mainsPowerFactorL1  PowerFactorDiv100,	-- 
	mainsPowerFactorL2  PowerFactorDiv100,	-- 
	mainsPowerFactorL3  PowerFactorDiv100,	-- 
	mainsAvgPowerFactor PowerFactorDiv100,	-- 
	mainsPhaseL1        Integer32,	        -- 
	mainsPhaseL2        Integer32,	        -- 
	mainsPhaseL3        Integer32,	        -- 
	mainsPhaseTotal     Integer32,	        -- 
	mainsVoltageLNAvg   VoltsLNDiv10,	    --
	mainsVoltageLNDiff  VoltsLNDiv10,	    --	    
	mainsVoltageLNMin   VoltsLNDiv10,	    --
	mainsVoltageLNMax   VoltsLNDiv10,	    --
	mainsVoltageLLAvg   VoltsLLDiv10,	    --
	mainsVoltageLLDiff  VoltsLLDiv10,	    --
	mainsVoltageLLMin   VoltsLLDiv10,	    --
	mainsVoltageLLMax   VoltsLLDiv10	    --
}

	genCurrentMin		CurrentDiv10,		--
	genCurrentMax		CurrentDiv10,		--
	genPowerTotalAvgPC  PowerPCDiv100,	    --

	genPowerTotalMinPC  PowerPCDiv10,	    -- 
	genPowerTotalMaxPC  PowerPCDiv10,	    --
